It is due to /usr/local/include/thrift/config.h:#define VERSION "0.9.3"
solution: change cassandra_constants.cpp  cassandra_constants.h
#pragma push_macro("VERSION")
#undef VERSION
namespace org { namespace apache { namespace cassandra {

class cassandraConstants {
 public:
  cassandraConstants();

  std::string VERSION;
};

extern const cassandraConstants g_cassandra_constants;

}}} // namespace
#pragma pop_macro("VERSION")
